                  <TR>
                    <TH WIDTH="300">Unit Narrative</TH>
                    <TH>Unit Roster</TH>
                  </TR>
                    <TD CLASS="ListItem1" VALIGN="TOP" style="padding: 5px;">WAR has a lengthy history dating back to MW3.<br>Our unit has evolved within the Mech Universe and it's ever demanding battle scenarios...WAR was primarily a close combat unit in it's earliest days BUT through the learning curves of League battles and pilot development WAR moved forward and evolved into a skilled unit in all types of mech combat.<br><br>Our pilots are a mixture of all nations, bringing Warriors from USA , Australia , Holland , Canada , Finland , Singapore, Germany & France. All of whom bring a certain quality and friendship that keep WAR's name a strong and respected one in the Mech Universe.<br><br>WAR shall always offer a strong and competitive battle to all those who challenge us in MWL , to whom we offer full respect in both Victory or Defeat.   <br><br>To become a member of WAR is to become part of an ongoing tradition of good friends, tough battles and a continuing involvement in the Mech Universe.<br><br>Strength, Honour and Fun to all!&nbsp;</TD>
